HTTP connection pool settings.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**h2UpgradePolicy**|"DEFAULT" | "DO_NOT_UPGRADE" | "UPGRADE"|Specify if http1.1 connection should be upgraded to http2 for the associated destination.<br /><br />Valid Options: DEFAULT, DO_NOT_UPGRADE, UPGRADE||
|**http1MaxPendingRequests**|int|Maximum number of requests that will be queued while waiting for a ready connection pool connection.||
|**http2MaxRequests**|int|Maximum number of active requests to a destination.||
|**idleTimeout**|str|The idle timeout for upstream connection pool connections.||
|**maxConcurrentStreams**|int|The maximum number of concurrent streams allowed for a peer on one HTTP/2 connection.||
|**maxRequestsPerConnection**|int|Maximum number of requests per connection to a backend.||
|**maxRetries**|int|Maximum number of retries that can be outstanding to all hosts in a cluster at a given time.||
|**useClientProtocol**|bool|If set to true, client protocol will be preserved while initiating connection to backend.||

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**connectTimeout**|str|TCP connection timeout.||
|**idleTimeout**|str|The idle timeout for TCP connections.||
|**maxConnectionDuration**|str|The maximum duration of a connection.||
|**maxConnections**|int|Maximum number of HTTP1 /TCP connections to a destination host.||
|**tcpKeepalive**|[NetworkingIstioIoV1DestinationRuleSpecSubsetsItems0TrafficPolicyPortLevelSettingsItems0ConnectionPoolTCPTCPKeepalive](#networkingistioiov1destinationrulespecsubsetsitems0trafficpolicyportlevelsettingsitems0connectionpooltcptcpkeepalive)|tcp keepalive||
### NetworkingIstioIoV1DestinationRuleSpecSubsetsItems0TrafficPolicyPortLevelSettingsItems0ConnectionPoolTCPTCPKeepalive

If set then set SO_KEEPALIVE on the socket to enable TCP Keepalives.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**interval**|str|The time duration between keep-alive probes.||
|**probes**|int|Maximum number of keepalive probes to send without response before deciding the connection is dead.||
|**time**|str|The time duration a connection needs to be idle before keep-alive probes start being sent.||

|**consecutiveErrors**|int|consecutive errors||
|**consecutiveGatewayErrors**|int|Number of gateway errors before a host is ejected from the connection pool.||
|**consecutiveLocalOriginFailures**|int|The number of consecutive locally originated failures before ejection occurs.||
|**interval**|str|Time interval between ejection sweep analysis.||
|**maxEjectionPercent**|int|Maximum % of hosts in the load balancing pool for the upstream service that can be ejected.||
|**minHealthPercent**|int|Outlier detection will be enabled as long as the associated load balancing pool has at least min_health_percent hosts in healthy mode.||
|**splitExternalLocalOriginErrors**|bool|Determines whether to distinguish local origin failures from external errors.||

### NetworkingIstioIoV1DestinationRuleSpecSubsetsItems0TrafficPolicyPortLevelSettingsItems0TLS

TLS related settings for connections to the upstream service.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**caCertificates**|str|OPTIONAL: The path to the file containing certificate authority certificates to use in verifying a presented server certificate.||
|**caCrl**|str|OPTIONAL: The path to the file containing the certificate revocation list (CRL) to use in verifying a presented server certificate.||
|**clientCertificate**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `MUTUAL`.||
|**credentialName**|str|The name of the secret that holds the TLS certs for the client including the CA certificates.||
|**insecureSkipVerify**|bool|`insecureSkipVerify` specifies whether the proxy should skip verifying the CA signature and SAN for the server certificate corresponding to the host.||
|**mode**|"DISABLE" | "SIMPLE" | "MUTUAL" | "ISTIO_MUTUAL"|Indicates whether connections to this port should be secured using TLS.<br /><br />Valid Options: DISABLE, SIMPLE, MUTUAL, ISTIO_MUTUAL||
|**privateKey**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `MUTUAL`.||
|**sni**|str|SNI string to present to the server during TLS handshake.||
|**subjectAltNames**|[str]|A list of alternate names to verify the subject identity in the certificate.||

|**maxRetries**|int|Maximum number of retries that can be outstanding to all hosts in a cluster at a given time.||

|**httpQueryParameterName**|str|Hash based on a specific HTTP query parameter.||

|**minimumRingSize**|int|Deprecated.||

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**caCertificates**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `MUTUAL` or `OPTIONAL_MUTUAL`.||

|**cipherSuites**|[str]|Optional: If specified, only support the specified cipher list.||
|**credentialName**|str|For gateways running on Kubernetes, the name of the secret that holds the TLS certs including the CA certificates.||
|**httpsRedirect**|bool|If set to true, the load balancer will send a 301 redirect for all http connections, asking the clients to use HTTPS.||
|**maxProtocolVersion**|"TLS_AUTO" | "TLSV1_0" | "TLSV1_1" | "TLSV1_2" | "TLSV1_3"|Optional: Maximum TLS protocol version.<br /><br />Valid Options: TLS_AUTO, TLSV1_0, TLSV1_1, TLSV1_2, TLSV1_3||

|**mode**|"PASSTHROUGH" | "SIMPLE" | "MUTUAL" | "AUTO_PASSTHROUGH" | "ISTIO_MUTUAL" | "OPTIONAL_MUTUAL"|Optional: Indicates whether connections to this port should be secured using TLS.<br /><br />Valid Options: PASSTHROUGH, SIMPLE, MUTUAL, AUTO_PASSTHROUGH, ISTIO_MUTUAL, OPTIONAL_MUTUAL||
|**privateKey**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `SIMPLE` or `MUTUAL`.||
|**serverCertificate**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `SIMPLE` or `MUTUAL`.||
|**subjectAltNames**|[str]|A list of alternate names to verify the subject identity in the certificate presented by the client.||
|**verifyCertificateHash**|[str]|An optional list of hex-encoded SHA-256 hashes of the authorized client certificates.||
|**verifyCertificateSpki**|[str]|An optional list of base64-encoded SHA-256 hashes of the SPKIs of authorized client certificates.||

|**serverCertificate**|str|REQUIRED if mode is `SIMPLE` or `MUTUAL`.||

|**verifyCertificateHash**|[str]|An optional list of hex-encoded SHA-256 hashes of the authorized client certificates.||
|**verifyCertificateSpki**|[str]|An optional list of base64-encoded SHA-256 hashes of the SPKIs of authorized client certificates.||

### NetworkingIstioIoV1VirtualServiceSpecHTTPItems0MatchItems0Authority

HTTP Authority values are case-sensitive and formatted as follows: - `exact: "value"` for exact string match - `prefix: "value"` for prefix-based match - `regex: "value"` for RE2 style regex-based match (https://github.com/google/re2/wiki/Syntax).

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**exact**|str|exact||
|**prefix**|str|prefix||
|**regex**|str|RE2 style regex-based match (https://github.com/google/re2/wiki/Syntax).||

### ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpec

Extend the functionality provided by the Istio proxy through WebAssembly filters. See more details at: https://istio.io/docs/reference/config/proxy_extensions/wasm-plugin.html

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**failStrategy**|"FAIL_CLOSE" | "FAIL_OPEN"|Specifies the failure behavior for the plugin due to fatal errors.<br /><br />Valid Options: FAIL_CLOSE, FAIL_OPEN||
|**imagePullPolicy**|"UNSPECIFIED_POLICY" | "IfNotPresent" | "Always"|The pull behaviour to be applied when fetching Wasm module by either OCI image or `http/https`.<br /><br />Valid Options: IfNotPresent, Always||
|**imagePullSecret**|str|Credentials to use for OCI image pulling.||
|**match**|[[ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpecMatchItems0](#extensionsistioiov1alpha1wasmpluginspecmatchitems0)]|Specifies the criteria to determine which traffic is passed to WasmPlugin.||
|**phase**|"UNSPECIFIED_PHASE" | "AUTHN" | "AUTHZ" | "STATS"|Determines where in the filter chain this `WasmPlugin` is to be injected.<br /><br />Valid Options: AUTHN, AUTHZ, STATS||
|**pluginConfig**|any|The configuration that will be passed on to the plugin.||
|**pluginName**|str|The plugin name to be used in the Envoy configuration (used to be called `rootID`).||
|**priority**|int|Determines ordering of `WasmPlugins` in the same `phase`.||
|**selector**|[ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpecSelector](#extensionsistioiov1alpha1wasmpluginspecselector)|selector||
|**sha256**|str|SHA256 checksum that will be used to verify Wasm module or OCI container.||
|**targetRef**|[ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpecTargetRef](#extensionsistioiov1alpha1wasmpluginspectargetref)|target ref||
|**targetRefs**|[[ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpecTargetRefsItems0](#extensionsistioiov1alpha1wasmpluginspectargetrefsitems0)]|Optional.||
|**type**|"UNSPECIFIED_PLUGIN_TYPE" | "HTTP" | "NETWORK"|||
|**url** `required`|str|URL of a Wasm module or OCI container.||
|**verificationKey**|str|verification key||
|**vmConfig**|[ExtensionsIstioIoV1alpha1WasmPluginSpecVMConfig](#extensionsistioiov1alpha1wasmpluginspecvmconfig)|vm config||

#### Attributes

|**context**|"ANY" | "SIDECAR_INBOUND" | "SIDECAR_OUTBOUND" | "GATEWAY"|The specific config generation context to match on.<br /><br />Valid Options: ANY, SIDECAR_INBOUND, SIDECAR_OUTBOUND, GATEWAY||
|**listener**|[NetworkingIstioIoV1alpha3EnvoyFilterSpecConfigPatchesItems0MatchListener](#networkingistioiov1alpha3envoyfilterspecconfigpatchesitems0matchlistener)|listener||
|**proxy**|[NetworkingIstioIoV1alpha3EnvoyFilterSpecConfigPatchesItems0MatchProxy](#networkingistioiov1alpha3envoyfilterspecconfigpatchesitems0matchproxy)|proxy||
|**routeConfiguration**|[NetworkingIstioIoV1alpha3EnvoyFilterSpecConfigPatchesItems0MatchRouteConfiguration](#networkingistioiov1alpha3envoyfilterspecconfigpatchesitems0matchrouteconfiguration)|route configuration||
